  <raw>Inside Alaska business



Mat-Su bureau seeks directors
The Mat-Su Convention and Visitors Bureau is seeking director nominations for three open seats on its 10-member board by today. Board members address CVB policy, political issues and serve as representatives for tourism in the Mat-Su area, working on a vision for the next 20 years. For details, contact Cheryl Metiva at bonnie@alaskavisit.com.


Alaska banks win high safety rating
Alaska banks and credit unions fared well in the latest round of safety scoring by bank rating agency Bauer Financial Inc. Bauer ranks banks and credit unions on a "five-star" scale, assessing their financial performance and strength.
Here are the rankings:
Five stars: First National Bank Alaska, Northrim Bank, Credit Union 1, Mt. McKinley Bank, Alaska Pacific Bank and Northern Skies Federal Credit Union.
Four stars: Wells Fargo Bank and the following credit unions -- Alaska USA, Denali Alaskan, Alaska District Engineers, Matanuska Valley, City of Fairbanks, Military and Civilian, Northern Schools, True North, ALPS and Tongass.
Three and a half stars: Alaska First Bank and Trust, Key Bank and Denali State Bank.

ACS Eagle River store moves
The Alaska Communications System store in Eagle River has relocated to 16707 Coronado St. The store is larger and will have on display ACS' high-speed wireless Internet service, letting customers try it on a laptop computer. The store's product displays also let customers browse without customer assistance, unlike the previous store, said spokeswoman Jeaneen Gill. The hours are 10 a.m. to 6 p.m. weekdays and 10 a.m. to 5 p.m. Saturdays.
-- Anchorage Daily News</raw>
